\index{wld\_rad\_getDiscoveryMethod@{wld\_rad\_getDiscoveryMethod}!wld\_radio.c@{wld\_radio.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wld\_rad\_getDiscoveryMethod()}{wld\_rad\_getDiscoveryMethod()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{wld_8h_a0f62a7362b1ffe0dbb87a26959e94be1}{wld\+\_\+ap\+\_\+dm\+\_\+m}} wld\+\_\+rad\+\_\+get\+Discovery\+Method (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{wld__types_8h_a495772ea52d0019034cc400feeffa0c3}{T\+\_\+\+Radio}} $\ast$}]{pR }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Return appropriate discovery method for one radio

If all APs are disabled, return DISABLED

If any AP is configured as NON default, it should configured the non default value of first AP

If all APs are configured as default then\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If 2.\+4 / 5GHz it returns RNR
\item If 6GHz, if any AP is not annouced in RNR on 2.\+4 or 5, return UPR otherwise DISABLED 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{wld__radio_8c_a4e9e1c96eb575ea8f8d6285ea1b86e9b}\label{wld__radio_8c_a4e9e1c96eb575ea8f8d6285ea1b86e9b}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wld\_rad\_hasOnlyActiveEP()}{wld\_rad\_hasOnlyActiveEP()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool wld\+\_\+rad\+\_\+has\+Only\+Active\+EP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{wld__types_8h_a495772ea52d0019034cc400feeffa0c3}{T\+\_\+\+Radio}} $\ast$}]{p\+Rad }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Function to check if ONLY an active End\+Point is present. In that case we can ignore some (AP) services as the Radio initial act as a passive device.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Rad} & -\/ Raido handler\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool -\/ TRUE when no active AP are found on this Radio wow pure EP, else FALSE. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
